  ### 4. COMPLETE TODO LIST
  1. **Install Python 3.7 (ensure it is the active Python version).**
     - On Ubuntu 22.04, Python 3.7 is not included by default. Install as follows:
       ```sh
       sudo apt-get update
       sudo apt-get install -y software-properties-common
       sudo add-apt-repository ppa:deadsnakes/ppa
       sudo apt-get update
       sudo apt-get install -y python3.7 python3.7-venv python3.7-dev
       ```
       - Verification: `python3.7 --version` should output Python 3.7.x.
  2. **Set up Python 3.7 as default for the project (optional but recommended for consistency):**
     - Use a virtual environment:
       ```sh
       python3.7 -m venv venv
       source venv/bin/activate
       ```
       - Verification: `which python` should point to the venv.
  3. **Install pip for Python 3.7 if not present:**
     - Inside venv:
       ```sh
       curl https://bootstrap.pypa.io/pip/3.7/get-pip.py -o get-pip.py
       python get-pip.py
       ```
       - Verification: `pip --version` references Python 3.7 site-packages.
  4. **Clone the repository via Git:**
     ```sh
     git clone https://github.com/rahulvigneswaran/Lottery-Ticket-Hypothesis-in-Pytorch.git /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Lottory
     cd /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Lottory
     ```
     - Verification: Directory structure matches README.md.
  5. **Upgrade pip:**
     ```sh
     pip install --upgrade pip
     ```
  6. **Install all Python dependencies exactly as pinned:**
     - Use a CPU-only PyTorch 1.2.0 wheel:
       ```sh
       pip install torch==1.2.0+cpu -f https://download.pytorch.org/whl/torch_stable.html
       pip install torchvision==0.4.0+cpu -f https://download.pytorch.org/whl/torch_stable.html
       pip install -r requirements.txt
       ```
       - Or, edit requirements.txt so torch and torchvision lines are `torch==1.2.0+cpu` and `torchvision==0.4.0+cpu` if using PyPI/extra-index-url.
     - **Do not install any CUDA or GPU packages.**
     - Verification: No install errors. Run:
       ```sh
       python -c "import torch, torchvision, matplotlib, seaborn, pandas, numpy, tensorboardX"
       ```
  7. **Skip CUDA Toolkit and all GPU-specific instructions.**
     - No CUDA install.
     - No NVIDIA drivers.
     - Remove any reference to `CUDA_VISIBLE_DEVICES` in `.env` or code.
     - Verification: `python -c "import torch; print(torch.cuda.is_available())"` prints `False`.
  8. **Create .env file only if needed for generic environment variables; do not include CUDA settings.**
  9. **Review and update .gitignore as needed.**
  10. **Verify requirements.txt matches exactly the provided list (CPU-only).**
      - If changes are made, repeat step 6.
      - Verification: Install in fresh venv.
  11. **(Optional) Create config.yaml or config.json if used.**

  14. **Run combine_plots.py after generating results.**

  #7 22.04 Description:
  #7 22.04 This PPA contains more recent Python versions packaged for Ubuntu.
  #7 22.04 
  #7 22.04 Disclaimer: there's no guarantee of timely updates in case of security problems or other issues. If you want to use them in a security-or-otherwise-critical environment (say, on a production server), you do so at your own risk.
  #7 22.04 
  #7 22.04 Update Note
  #7 22.04 ===========
  #7 22.04 Please use this repository instead of ppa:fkrull/deadsnakes.
  #7 22.04 
  #7 22.04 Reporting Issues
  #7 22.04 ================
  #7 22.04 
  #7 22.04 Issues can be reported in the master issue tracker at:
  #7 22.04 https://github.com/deadsnakes/issues/issues
  #7 22.04 
  #7 22.04 Supported Ubuntu and Python Versions
  #7 22.04 ====================================
  #7 22.04 
  #7 22.04 - Ubuntu 20.04 (focal) Python3.5 - Python3.7, Python3.9 - Python3.13
  #7 22.04 - Ubuntu 22.04 (jammy) Python3.7 - Python3.9, Python3.11 - Python3.13
  #7 22.04 - Ubuntu 24.04 (noble) Python3.7 - Python3.11, Python3.13
  #7 22.04 - Note: Python2.7 (focal, jammy), Python 3.8 (focal), Python 3.10 (jammy), Python3.12 (noble) are not provided by deadsnakes as upstream ubuntu provides those packages.
  #7 22.04 
  #7 22.04 Why some packages aren't built:
  #7 22.04 - Note: for focal, older python versions require libssl<1.1 so they are not currently built
  #7 22.04 - Note: for jammy and noble, older python versions requre libssl<3 so they are not currently built
  #7 22.04 - If you need these, reach out to asottile to set up a private ppa
  #7 22.04 
  #7 22.04 The packages may also work on other versions of Ubuntu or Debian, but that is not tested or supported.
  #7 22.04 
  #7 22.04 Packages
  #7 22.04 ========
  #7 22.04 
  #7 22.04 The packages provided here are loosely based on the debian upstream packages with some modifications to make them more usable as non-default pythons and on ubuntu.  As such, the packages follow debian's patterns and often do not include a full python distribution with just `apt install python#.#`.  Here is a list of packages that may be useful along with the default install:
  #7 22.04 
  #7 22.04 - `python#.#-dev`: includes development headers for building C extensions
  #7 22.04 - `python#.#-venv`: provides the standard library `venv` module
  #7 22.04 - `python#.#-distutils`: provides the standard library `distutils` module
  #7 22.04 - `python#.#-lib2to3`: provides the `2to3-#.#` utility as well as the standard library `lib2to3` module
  #7 22.04 - `python#.#-gdbm`: provides the standard library `dbm.gnu` module
  #7 22.04 - `python#.#-tk`: provides the standard library `tkinter` module
  #7 22.04 
  #7 22.04 Third-Party Python Modules
  #7 22.04 ==========================
  #7 22.04 
  #7 22.04 Python modules in the official Ubuntu repositories are packaged to work with the Python interpreters from the official repositories. Accordingly, they generally won't work with the Python interpreters from this PPA. As an exception, pure-Python modules for Python 3 will work, but any compiled extension modules won't.
  #7 22.04 
  #7 22.04 To install 3rd-party Python modules, you should use the common Python packaging tools.  For an introduction into the Python packaging ecosystem and its tools, refer to the Python Packaging User Guide:
  #7 22.04 https://packaging.python.org/installing/
  #7 22.04 
  #7 22.04 Sources
  #7 22.04 =======
  #7 22.04 The package sources are available at:
  #7 22.04 https://github.com/deadsnakes/

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM --platform=linux/amd64 ubuntu:22.04
  # Set non-interactive frontend for apt
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  # Set the working directory as required
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Lottory
  # Install dependencies for adding PPAs, Python build, and common tools
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          software-properties-common \
          build-essential \
          curl \
          wget \
          git \
          ca-certificates \
          libssl-dev \
          libffi-dev \
          libbz2-dev \
          libreadline-dev \
          libsqlite3-dev \
          zlib1g-dev \
          libncurses5-dev \
          libgdbm-dev \
          libnss3-dev \
          liblzma-dev \
          python3-pip \
          python3-setuptools \
          python3-distutils \
          python3-venv && \
      add-apt-repository ppa:deadsnakes/ppa && \
      apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          python3.7 \
          python3.7-venv \
          python3.7-dev && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install pip for Python 3.7
  RUN curl https://bootstrap.pypa.io/pip/3.7/get-pip.py -o /tmp/get-pip.py && \
      python3.7 /tmp/get-pip.py && \
      rm /tmp/get-pip.py
  # Ensure pip and virtualenv are upgraded for Python 3.7
  RUN python3.7 -m pip install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel
  # Clone the repository
  RUN git clone https://github.com/rahulvigneswaran/Lottery-Ticket-Hypothesis-in-Pytorch.git /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Lottory
  # Copy requirements.txt to ensure strict version pins before install
  COPY requirements.txt /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Lottory/requirements.txt
  # Create a virtual environment with Python 3.7 and activate it
  RUN python3.7 -m venv /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Lottory/venv
  # Install torch and torchvision (CPU-only versions), then other requirements
  RUN . /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Lottory/venv/bin/activate && \
      python --version && \
      pip install --upgrade pip && \
      pip install torch==1.2.0+cpu torchvision==0.4.0+cpu -f https://download.pytorch.org/whl/torch_stable.html && \
      pip install -r requirements.txt
  # Set environment variables to use the venv Python and pip by default
  ENV VIRTUAL_ENV=/home/cc/EnvGym/data/Lottory/venv
  ENV PATH="$VIRTUAL_ENV/bin:$PATH"
  # Default command: bash shell
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 1 ---

  #7 2.530 
  #7 2.530 Supported Ubuntu and Python Versions
  #7 2.530 ====================================
  #7 2.530 
  #7 2.530 - Ubuntu 20.04 (focal) Python3.5 - Python3.7, Python3.9 - Python3.13
  #7 2.530 - Ubuntu 22.04 (jammy) Python3.7 - Python3.9, Python3.11 - Python3.13
  #7 2.530 - Ubuntu 24.04 (noble) Python3.7 - Python3.11, Python3.13
  #7 2.530 - Note: Python2.7 (focal, jammy), Python 3.8 (focal), Python 3.10 (jammy), Python3.12 (noble) are not provided by deadsnakes as upstream ubuntu provides those packages.
  #7 2.530 
  #7 2.530 Why some packages aren't built:
  #7 2.530 - Note: for focal, older python versions require libssl<1.1 so they are not currently built
  #7 2.530 - Note: for jammy and noble, older python versions requre libssl<3 so they are not currently built
  #7 2.530 - If you need these, reach out to asottile to set up a private ppa
  #7 2.530 
  #7 2.530 The packages may also work on other versions of Ubuntu or Debian, but that is not tested or supported.
  #7 2.530 
  #7 2.530 Packages
  #7 2.530 ========
  #7 2.530 
  #7 2.530 The packages provided here are loosely based on the debian upstream packages with some modifications to make them more usable as non-default pythons and on ubuntu.  As such, the packages follow debian's patterns and often do not include a full python distribution with just `apt install python#.#`.  Here is a list of packages that may be useful along with the default install:
  #7 2.530 
  #7 2.530 - `python#.#-dev`: includes development headers for building C extensions
  #7 2.530 - `python#.#-venv`: provides the standard library `venv` module
  #7 2.530 - `python#.#-distutils`: provides the standard library `distutils` module
  #7 2.530 - `python#.#-lib2to3`: provides the `2to3-#.#` utility as well as the standard library `lib2to3` module
  #7 2.530 - `python#.#-gdbm`: provides the standard library `dbm.gnu` module
  #7 2.530 - `python#.#-tk`: provides the standard library `tkinter` module
  #7 2.530 
  #7 2.530 Third-Party Python Modules
  #7 2.530 ==========================
  #7 2.530 
  #7 2.530 Python modules in the official Ubuntu repositories are packaged to work with the Python interpreters from the official repositories. Accordingly, they generally won't work with the Python interpreters from this PPA. As an exception, pure-Python modules for Python 3 will work, but any compiled extension modules won't.
  #7 2.530 
  #7 2.530 To install 3rd-party Python modules, you should use the common Python packaging tools.  For an introduction into the Python packaging ecosystem and its tools, refer to the Python Packaging User Guide:
  #7 2.530 https://packaging.python.org/installing/
  #7 2.530

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM --platform=linux/amd64 ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Lottory
  # Step 1: Install software-properties-common and ca-certificates to enable add-apt-repository
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          software-properties-common \
          ca-certificates && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Step 2: Add deadsnakes PPA for Python 3.7
  RUN add-apt-repository ppa:deadsnakes/ppa && \
      apt-get update
  # Step 3: Install remaining dependencies and Python 3.7
  RUN apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          build-essential \
          curl \
          wget \
          git \
          libssl-dev \
          libffi-dev \
          libbz2-dev \
          libreadline-dev \
          libsqlite3-dev \
          zlib1g-dev \
          libncurses5-dev \
          libgdbm-dev \
          libnss3-dev \
          liblzma-dev \
          python3-pip \
          python3-setuptools \
          python3-distutils \
          python3-venv \
          python3.7 \
          python3.7-venv \
          python3.7-dev && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install pip for Python 3.7
  RUN curl https://bootstrap.pypa.io/pip/3.7/get-pip.py -o /tmp/get-pip.py && \
      python3.7 /tmp/get-pip.py && \
      rm /tmp/get-pip.py
  RUN python3.7 -m pip install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel
  # Clone the repository
  RUN git clone https://github.com/rahulvigneswaran/Lottery-Ticket-Hypothesis-in-Pytorch.git /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Lottory
  # Use requirements.txt from the cloned repo (since it exists in directory tree)
  RUN python3.7 -m venv /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Lottory/venv
  RUN . /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Lottory/venv/bin/activate && \
      python --version && \
      pip install --upgrade pip && \
      pip install torch==1.2.0+cpu torchvision==0.4.0+cpu -f https://download.pytorch.org/whl/torch_stable.html && \
      pip install -r requirements.txt
  ENV VIRTUAL_ENV=/home/cc/EnvGym/data/Lottory/venv
  ENV PATH="$VIRTUAL_ENV/bin:$PATH"
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  #7 6.556 Repository: 'deb https://ppa.launchpadcontent.net/deadsnakes/ppa/ubuntu/ jammy main'
  #7 6.556 Description:
  #7 6.556 This PPA contains more recent Python versions packaged for Ubuntu.
  #7 6.556 
  #7 6.556 Disclaimer: there's no guarantee of timely updates in case of security problems or other issues. If you want to use them in a security-or-otherwise-critical environment (say, on a production server), you do so at your own risk.
  #7 6.556 
  #7 6.556 Update Note
  #7 6.556 ===========
  #7 6.556 Please use this repository instead of ppa:fkrull/deadsnakes.
  #7 6.556 
  #7 6.556 Reporting Issues
  #7 6.556 ================
  #7 6.556 
  #7 6.556 Issues can be reported in the master issue tracker at:
  #7 6.556 https://github.com/deadsnakes/issues/issues
  #7 6.556 
  #7 6.556 Supported Ubuntu and Python Versions
  #7 6.556 ====================================
  #7 6.556 
  #7 6.556 - Ubuntu 20.04 (focal) Python3.5 - Python3.7, Python3.9 - Python3.13
  #7 6.556 - Ubuntu 22.04 (jammy) Python3.7 - Python3.9, Python3.11 - Python3.13
  #7 6.556 - Ubuntu 24.04 (noble) Python3.7 - Python3.11, Python3.13
  #7 6.556 - Note: Python2.7 (focal, jammy), Python 3.8 (focal), Python 3.10 (jammy), Python3.12 (noble) are not provided by deadsnakes as upstream ubuntu provides those packages.
  #7 6.556 
  #7 6.556 Why some packages aren't built:
  #7 6.556 - Note: for focal, older python versions require libssl<1.1 so they are not currently built
  #7 6.556 - Note: for jammy and noble, older python versions requre libssl<3 so they are not currently built
  #7 6.556 - If you need these, reach out to asottile to set up a private ppa
  #7 6.556 
  #7 6.556 The packages may also work on other versions of Ubuntu or Debian, but that is not tested or supported.
  #7 6.556 
  #7 6.556 Packages
  #7 6.556 ========
  #7 6.556 
  #7 6.556 The packages provided here are loosely based on the debian upstream packages with some modifications to make them more usable as non-default pythons and on ubuntu.  As such, the packages follow debian's patterns and often do not include a full python distribution with just `apt install python#.#`.  Here is a list of packages that may be useful along with the default install:
  #7 6.556 
  #7 6.556 - `python#.#-dev`: includes development headers for building C extensions
  #7 6.556 - `python#.#-venv`: provides the standard library `venv` module
  #7 6.556 - `python#.#-distutils`: provides the standard library `distutils` module
  #7 6.556 - `python#.#-lib2to3`: provides the `2to3-#.#` utility as well as the standard library `lib2to3` module
  #7 6.556 - `python#.#-gdbm`: provides the standard library `dbm.gnu` module
  #7 6.556 - `python#.#-tk`: provides the standard library `tkinter` module
  #7 6.556 
  #7 6.556 Third-Party Python Modules
  #7 6.556 ==========================
  #7 6.556 
  #7 6.556 Python modules in the official Ubuntu repositories are packaged to work with the Python interpreters from the official repositories. Accordingly, they generally won't work with the Python interpreters from this PPA. As an exception, pure-Python modules for Python 3 will work, but any compiled extension modules won't.
  #7 6.556 
  #7 6.556 To install 3rd-party Python modules, you should use the common Python packaging tools.  For an introduction into the Python packaging ecosystem and its tools, refer to the Python Packaging User Guide:
  #7 6.556 https://packaging.python.org/installing/
  #7 6.556

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM --platform=linux/amd64 ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Lottory
  # Step 1: Install software-properties-common, ca-certificates, lsb-release, and gnupg to enable add-apt-repository
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          software-properties-common \
          ca-certificates \
          lsb-release \
          gnupg && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Step 2: Add deadsnakes PPA for Python 3.7
  RUN add-apt-repository ppa:deadsnakes/ppa && \
      apt-get update
  # Step 3: Install remaining dependencies and Python 3.7
  RUN apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          build-essential \
          curl \
          wget \
          git \
          libssl-dev \
          libffi-dev \
          libbz2-dev \
          libreadline-dev \
          libsqlite3-dev \
          zlib1g-dev \
          libncurses5-dev \
          libgdbm-dev \
          libnss3-dev \
          liblzma-dev \
          python3-pip \
          python3-setuptools \
          python3-distutils \
          python3-venv \
          python3.7 \
          python3.7-venv \
          python3.7-dev && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install pip for Python 3.7
  RUN curl https://bootstrap.pypa.io/pip/3.7/get-pip.py -o /tmp/get-pip.py && \
      python3.7 /tmp/get-pip.py && \
      rm /tmp/get-pip.py
  RUN python3.7 -m pip install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel
  # Clone the repository
  RUN git clone https://github.com/rahulvigneswaran/Lottery-Ticket-Hypothesis-in-Pytorch.git /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Lottory
  # Use requirements.txt from the cloned repo (since it exists in directory tree)
  RUN python3.7 -m venv /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Lottory/venv
  RUN . /home/cc/EnvGym/data/Lottory/venv/bin/activate && \
      python --version && \
      pip install --upgrade pip && \
      pip install torch==1.2.0+cpu torchvision==0.4.0+cpu -f https://download.pytorch.org/whl/torch_stable.html && \
      pip install -r requirements.txt
  ENV VIRTUAL_ENV=/home/cc/EnvGym/data/Lottory/venv
  ENV PATH="$VIRTUAL_ENV/bin:$PATH"
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
